Connected by Time and Destiny
You all are walking the path of life, having grown from the age of infancy through childhood. The formation of a nation is similar. It begins from the very start and grows toward a certain purpose through various stages of development. Our Unification Church is the same. The Unification Church has been born and is growing. From this perspective, the question is which person, which nation, or which religion becomes great. 
 The Power of Love as the Driving Force of All Strength
For a person to succeed, their purpose must be clear. The purpose must be certain. If one zigzags up and down along the way, it results in a waste of time. It brings about a consumption of time. When you study, from elementary school to middle school, high school, and university, going through bachelor’s and doctoral courses, what you major in is an extremely important issue. 
From this viewpoint, if you put in more effort during the elementary school years, you can reach a position where you can enter middle school. To reach the master's course, it takes about 18 to 19 years, and for the doctoral course, it takes about 20 to 21 years. While the duration of study is set, the question of how to compress this in terms of time requires a doubling of effort. 
Whether you shorten that period to 18 years or 10 years depends on whom? It is not limited by time; it depends on you. Time should not dominate you; you must become someone who can dominate time. Isn’t that right? 
To go toward a certain purpose, a certain amount of time is necessary. Also, there is a certain time, and one must invest a certain amount of effort during that time. Furthermore, even if you invest a certain amount of effort in a certain time, the difference lies in how much sincerity you put into it. How much do you unite your body and mind in that effort? 
Then, where do you get the strength to put in that sincerity and all your energy? That is the question. You stand in two positions: whether you receive support from external forces or whether you maintain your own subjectivity through your own strength. There are these two paths, and the question is which path is more effective. It is necessary to have this intrinsic driving force so that you can proceed without relying on anyone’s external cooperation. 
Now, what is the most necessary thing for having this intrinsic driving force? What should be the core of that motivation? There may be external things like money or success, but from the emotional aspect, the way to maintain your subjectivity is through a foundation of long-term sincerity, which we can deduce from a very common-sense perspective. 
This high-level love, where does such explosive driving force come from? It must arise from relative relationships, such as between parents and children, or between lovers. It revolves around these relative relationships. Where do you receive such explosive stimulation? You receive it from love. However, love also varies depending on the situation. Is the environment good or bad for each other? How about you? 
In a bad environment, the shock received through love can serve as a standard that possesses an unchanging driving force. Isn’t that more valuable? Isn’t it more rewarding? 
For example, if parents who care deeply for their child want them to do certain things, but the child cannot think of everything the parents hoped for and taught, let’s say they received it anyway. However, if the parents were unjustly sacrificed and killed by someone who is an enemy, perhaps a lawyer or a professor, and if they were falsely accused and killed, that can become a shock that leads the child to resolve, 'I must surpass them in ten years.' If that determination arises, it can create a path for the child to put forth all their effort and sincerity to surpass the enemy and take revenge on behalf of their parents. 
Also, if there are two people in love but they are placed in a situation where they cannot fulfill that love due to opposition, if they resolve to overcome that together, that determination can create a path to overcome all obstacles. We see this often in society and daily life. 
 The Development of Religion Through Martyrdom
If we elevate that to a higher level, it is the same when fighting for the country and its independence. If a patriot sees their people suffering and being killed in a miserable environment, the more they see it, the more they will unite and strive to change the nation that inflicts such harm. If they resolve to do so, we cannot help but think that the love that serves as the condition for that resolution can lead to a quicker path to achieving their purpose. 
In this light, a religion is no different. God is the same. God also wants to proceed quickly toward a certain purpose. From that perspective, how should one proceed? Should one go through a good environment that is welcomed by everyone, or should one go through a persecuted and difficult environment? 
There is a set purpose to be achieved, and even if that purpose is clearly established, one must stand in a position of internal unity and determination against those who oppose that purpose. The more victims there are, the stronger the persecution, the stronger one must be, rather than retreating. 
As you know, during a war, when occupying a hill, even a small hill requires a large number of troops, and if all comrades bleed and die, if there is love for those comrades, the more love there is, the more there will be a counter-reaction to retake that hill rather than retreat. 
When we see this, why has God allowed Christianity and all religions to be sacrificed and shed blood? It can be seen as a strategy to ignite the fire of love. It is not ordinary; it demands a powerful and unchanging explosive love. Thus, in the path of a religion that faces persecution and death, the connections and motivations for explosive love can sprout. 
Why is that? Because the love for comrades or the power to love one’s purpose completely explodes. The history of martyrdom in religious history, which has not existed in general history, was a strategy by God to evoke a higher level of motivation than what ordinary humans seek in love. 
Then, comrades leave their last words. 'Please understand my intentions and fulfill my wishes.' The more people there are who love, the more serious it becomes. Just thinking about it brings tears to the eyes. Therefore, how can one catch that continuous environment that makes it hard to sleep? Isn’t it better to have one comrade with such determination than to be alone? 
From this perspective, why do we believe in religion? Wouldn’t it be better to believe in friends instead of religion? God is a subject who always treats those who pledge loyalty and risk their lives for a public purpose from a subjective position. When I shed tears and struggle, God sheds even more tears and struggles as a subject. When one is consumed with the heart of public love, God is the center of love and the subject, so He always responds to the heart stimulated by love and supplies the driving force necessary to achieve that purpose. 
To fulfill that purpose centered on love, a co-worker is needed, but if there are no such co-workers in the world, how happy would it be if God could be that co-worker? 
That God is better than a father. Better than parents. Better than brothers. Better than any teacher or anyone who loves you. If you know that fact, how grateful that being is. To receive encouragement from such a being, 'You will surely succeed if you go this way. No matter what difficulties you face, if you go this way, you will succeed,' how shocking would that be? If you know that, how much sincerity would you put in, and how much would you struggle? 
Centered on the heart of love, even if one sacrifices oneself, to achieve a public purpose of love for loved ones, in that position, God actively works even harder than oneself. If that happens, if enemies are watching you and teaching you how to proceed, saying, 'You must go this way,' could you give that up? "No," it cannot be done. 
Therefore, in receiving the power of love’s impulse to achieve some great purpose, I find that the most unchanging and always relevant subject to me is God, and I want to connect that God into my living sphere. That life is religious life. Thus, God is a subject who can explode such love and supply the driving force to achieve that public purpose. 
 God in a Serious and Tense Position
So, does God prefer to discuss things in an ordinary setting, or does He prefer to discuss things in a serious and tense setting? Also, when God listens to prayers, does He listen to ordinary prayers, or does He listen to serious prayers made in a setting where the whole world holds its breath? Have you ever experienced that? 
Do you know what acceleration is? God is the one who accelerates and speeds things up. The more you go, the faster the speed increases. When you do something, do you prefer to do it quickly or slowly? "Quickly." Then, does He say, 'Hey, take a break there,' or does He push you hard, saying, 'You little rascals'? He doesn’t tell you to rest. 
Look, those who walk slowly and clumsily will fall if someone kicks them from behind, but those who are quick and nimble will move quickly. What type do you want to be? "The second one." Push me. Just hit it like playing golf! I will fly! (Laughter) What do you want to be? If you are not prepared, you will flatten out. 
The ball, no matter how much you hit it, will always return to its original shape. It will always return to its original position. That is the nature of the ball. You use that. Are you the same? "Yes." Are you the type that flattens out and changes after one hit, or are you the type that does not change? "I am the type that does not change." (Laughter) That sounds good. It should be that way. No matter how much you suffer or face persecution, you should not change. You must not change, and because of that, you should become stronger. 
When you go to a soccer field, you kick the ball, right? You receive the incoming ball with your head, and like this… (gesturing while speaking) Would the ball dislike that? It is its mission. (Laughter) The more you receive and kick, the more likely your side is to win. When the ball is coming from over there and there is a keeper here, will the ball say, 'Hey, let’s have a nice collision with your foot'? Or will it say, 'Oh no! Your foot is scary'? Will it want to be kicked weakly or strongly? "Strongly." That’s right. 
God is the same. God is a stimulating God. I have come to realize that God likes new things. He always likes new things. He dislikes old things. Also, He is not one-sided. He is diverse. 
When you look at a masterpiece, do you just say, 'Oh, this is a good masterpiece' with just one cut? It must have a variety of colors and harmonies that create a beauty that can be appreciated by both old and young, and that is what makes it a masterpiece. 
So, do you need God? "Yes." Why? Why? In an ordinary path, you do not need God. Are you serious people? "Yes." Are you really serious people? "Yes." What is serious? What makes you serious? You need to know that. It is because you have lost love that you are serious. I was the owner of love that could not be changed even if I gave this world or the entire universe, but I am serious because I have been robbed of that love and lost it. 
This enemy called Satan has not only taken our parents but has killed our father, violated our mother, and done all this… With the mother taken away, he has cut off the heads of all the siblings. You must understand that. Therefore, we must repay the enemy of our father and the enemies of our siblings.
You have the responsibility to repay the debts and avenge your mother’s enemies. Such a shock...

The closer you get to God, the more you will experience that provocative love. It's not just words; it's a fact. Are you serious? What are you all doing here? Why did you come so early in the morning? You came to receive the stimulation to go on the shortcut of avenging the enemies of God's love.

So, in the context of the Unification Church, Reverend Moon being chased and persecuted is not different. Because he knows the path of corruption, he understands that people fell due to love... Everyone has become an enemy.

Even if it is difficult for the teacher to take on such responsibilities, even if countless enemies appear... That’s why we talk about connections. 

We have the responsibility to repay the enemies of God's love. 

So, where do we meet these enemies that we need to repay? If they come personally, we must meet them personally. We need to know that the enemy is targeting me at some crossroads and we must confront them. The enemy is targeting families, society, tribes, nations, and is lurking at every intersection. Therefore, such tragedies will occur in my family, if I lead the church, there will be life and death situations in the church, and if I lead the nation, there will be life and death situations in the nation, and when it comes to the world, there must be such crossroads.

Then Satan will launch a full-scale attack. Do you understand what I mean? Even if you enter a place of death, you cannot even dream of thinking that you will not die. Do you have that kind of heart? "Yes." Even if you enter a place of fatigue, if you only have that thought...

How should the members of the Unification Church interact with each other? For the purpose, the entire Unification Church walks a miserable path, and the more miserable it is, the more they can encourage each other, the more unified that organization becomes. The suffering you are going through is an effort to find a more valuable love. A more valuable love...

I started working in earnest in the U.S. from 1973. If there is Satan, Reverend Moon cannot remain still. Therefore, an attack is inevitable. That’s why on the day I fall, I will leave behind the words that I fell because of heavenly love, not because of anything else. I am not falling because I covet American money. I am not falling because I covet power. I am doing this to find God's love. Therefore, it is a real fight. Do you understand? Are you like that? "Yes."

In this fight, if you win, you can find the wife you lost from heaven, you can find your family, you can find your parents, you can find your nation and everything, but on the day you lose this fight, you will lose everything, and everything you have sworn and worked for until now will return to nothing. We have the mission to repay the enemies of love.

The enemies of love, the enemies of the father, the enemies of the brothers, repaying the enemies that have destroyed the ideal love garden is in my hands and is my responsibility, and when I think of that, it is serious. Therefore, there is nowhere I can refrain from touching. I do not like the leaders of the Unification Church. The enemies of love... That is why everything is serious...

When Reverend Moon tries to engage in the fishing business, there is a lot of fuss about it. Also, there is a lot of fuss about trying to make movies these days. Why is that? What others do is not a problem, but why is it a fuss when I do it? (Laughter) Because I am trying to repay the enemies of love. Because I am trying to take away the foundation of the satanic world. With that thought, the teacher is pouring his whole life into this. So, he has set aside 21 years to settle all fights during this period.

He is doing a great task that no one in history has ever done. For the past 20 years, the world has been in chaos. Even the United States, the center of the democratic world, has fallen from the top, and communists have fallen, and Christians have fallen from high places, and now it is chaos. Do you know why? Because it is the period to repay the enemies of love on a global scale. Everything depends on that.

So, will God cooperate or not? "He will." Nowadays, the position of white people in America, during World War II, shone like the sun, but now it is like a falling star, right? Do you understand what I mean?

Otherwise, would Reverend Moon come here to work? Think about it. Would I be able to work if the habits of dealing with Asian people and Chinese people from 50 years ago remained unchanged? Do you understand? Back then, they didn’t treat us like anything. They fed their own dogs at home, but they wouldn’t even let Asians enter their rooms. Do you know that fact? That is a historical fact. Isn’t that true?

If that is the case, would Reverend Moon come here to work? Think about it. When I came to America, the same things were happening. It’s the same. So, let’s all fight globally! Let’s come out and fight! This fight is actually one I created. In a short time, from Lincoln Center to Madison Square Garden, Yankee Stadium, and the Washington rally, I made explosive noise. That is not an easy task. In a short time, sweeping across America, the one who caused problems, regardless of who it is, is more famous than anyone in history, more than the president. That is why there is opposition to Reverend Moon. They say he is not capable, yet they are interested. (Applause)

Yesterday, I gathered about 70 or 80 frontier leaders for a meeting, and I heard that they have a lot of interest in the Unification Church, but even more interest in the teacher. When the teacher comes out, the entire media... And they say they don’t need the teacher, they only need themselves. (Applause) Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is opposed, but because the members of the Unification Church are walking the path of true love, they cannot help but be interested. Have you all become like that? "Yes." Is that really true? "Yes."

The people who oppose us, when everyone else is sleeping in the early morning, Reverend Moon of the Unification Church says, "Gather at 5:30," and when the young people of the Unification Church gather, everyone else is snoring, and they say that no matter what you ask, they don’t respond. They just sit here and sleep. (Laughter) How happy would the great Satan be to see that? Do you know that? "Yes."

All members of the Unification Church should carry a syringe. And when they are dozing off, they should just close their eyes and stab themselves in the butt with the syringe. Now, is this stabbing love, or is leaving them alone love? (Applause) Why? For the prestige of our Unification Church... When they see that, how does Satan feel?

Why do I call everyone to gather in the early morning when others are sleeping? The satanic world is night. The opposing ones oppose after 10 PM. They need to sleep; they don’t even have the energy to oppose. So, I think this time is the most empty period. The opposing faction is lazy, so we all gather to worship, and they think that the Unification Church doesn’t even gather on Sundays. You need to understand that. We are always in that fight.

What fight is it? It is the fight to repay the enemies of love. You must understand that we have joined this holy fight to repay the historical enemies who have violated the love of humanity and the love of God throughout history.

We are at the forefront of repaying God's enemies. 

If I keep talking like this, it will never end. What time is it now? It is 7:15. What time is it? "Ten minutes." Ten minutes? Let’s do a little more. Do you understand? What kind of connection do we have? We have a connection to repay the enemies of love. We must repay the enemies of love. The enemies of our mother’s love, the enemies of our father’s love, the enemies of God’s love, the enemies of our brothers’ love, the enemies of the love of our nation’s people, the enemies of love in the universe, and the enemies of love in the kingdom of heaven. Let’s repay those enemies. There is only one enemy. Do you understand? "Yes."

If you are trying to repay even one person’s enemy, how can you leave the common historical enemy that has come down through thousands of years centered on God and humanity? Should we just leave that enemy alone? Should we repay that enemy or not? "We must repay." How much should we repay? When you think about that, even if you say 'yes,' it still doesn’t connect. But can life be like this? The way of eating, dressing, and living must be changed to repay the enemies. Therefore, this place is always serious because it is a place where we can meet the enemies.

I came to meet the enemy that represents the world, so it is always serious. I came to America to meet the enemy that represents the world. This country is currently trying to ruin the world as a representative nation. You must understand how much influence this situation in America has on young men and women worldwide. What is free sex? What is streaking? So here, they say not to even hold hands. Men only hold hands with men. They do not do what Satan likes. This is a place to repay the enemies of Satan. Do you understand? "Yes."

Here in America, I am waging a counter-offensive against God’s enemies and humanity’s enemies. We, who were born with such connections, are the enemies of God’s love in this era, and we were born with a shared destiny for the enemies who have violated all historical love.

In Korea, the country has despised us, in Japan, the country has opposed us, and in America, the country has opposed us. But even if the whole world opposes us, we must repay God’s enemies. We cannot fail here. That is why, even when we pray, we cry out, "Father! Here I am." You must understand that.

The providence of God in history and reality

The teacher is not someone who lives comfortably or just does things moderately. I hear the church bells at one o'clock, two o'clock, and three o'clock while I sleep. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Just like I do this, you all must do the same. If I repay the enemies like this, you must carry on the legacy well.

For victory, I could forget about eating and sleeping as much as I needed. God is greater than me. God has suffered more than I have. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

I could not be in a position to enjoy myself, nor could I be in a position to sing joyfully. I could not be in a position to dance and play. If I were to set a sign at my grave when I die, I would want it to say, "Reverend Moon repaid all the enemies of God’s love." Reverend Moon holding the Washington rally and doing this and that is all unnecessary. That is just a means to repay God’s love. Do you understand? "Yes." In this endeavor, how serious I am and how much sincerity I put into that purpose will be the shortcut to the kingdom of heaven...

So, when I read books, I read books about war and books that have spies. The same goes for movies. I do not watch sad stories, love stories, or stories about men and women. Above all scenes, I have the responsibility to repay the enemies of love.

Think about it. After Satan caused the fall of Adam's family, God was working through Abel, but he disrupted that as well. Noah prepared his family for 120 years, but through Ham, he also caused Noah's fall. When Abraham was about to offer a sacrifice at the altar, he disrupted that too, and he disrupted Moses as well. You must understand that we must fight against the champion Satan who has disrupted everything throughout history.
The global persecution era against the Unification Church began in 1976. That was the peak, you know? Nowadays, it's quiet, right? Even those who used to talk about Reverend Moon are all quiet these days. Isn't that right? "Yes." The struggle centered around the Washington Conference was intense. You all don't know how serious it was for the teacher.

I go out to sea on a boat, but it's not just for fun. These foolish ones go in and sleep soundly. What is sleep? Those who don't understand are sleeping. Do you know what that means? That's right. If the Washington Conference fails, it would be better for me to die. The Washington Conference was more serious than a death row inmate going to the execution ground. It's like betting the world on a gambling table and drawing the last card. Would I forget 1976 in my life? Would I forget the fact that it rained during the Yankee Stadium event? "No." I can't forget it. And with that, I made an enormous resolution within 80 days and declared the Washington Conference. I did it with my life on the line. You have no idea how serious it was then. That was not something a person did. If it were a person, it would have failed one hundred percent.

So what happens if it fails? It would be shocking for Reverend Moon. Then how would the dignity of heaven be affected, and how would the fate of the entire Unification Church be determined? I know well, and heaven knows well, that heaven could not help but mobilize. So it ended completely successfully, without any accidents, and everything we did became a historical record.

So now we are moving into a three-year phase after finishing the Washington Conference. After completing the second year... Do you understand? Everything that was an issue in the National Assembly will be finished by September. When that happens, no matter how much they investigate, they won't do anything. Even if we ask them to investigate, they won't do it. At that time, even if Reverend Moon actually killed someone, they wouldn't believe it. It's all just rumors, and I don't believe them either. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Our mission is to stand on the final battlefield to repay the enemies of love. Standing on the final battlefield, we are finding a way to determine our fate. The Unification Church members are on the front line. In this unprecedented war in history, will you be a veteran or a non-combatant? "Veteran..." If I have a machine gun, will I shoot it? Will I take all the bullets? Or will I just watch and appreciate? Will I fight while bleeding and breaking my legs? Will you fight? "Yes." Why? Because we know that our loved ones have died in a more miserable way, have been sacrificed miserably. I have received a heavenly mission to instill such thoughts in you. So I will mobilize the nation and the world with my own hands to create veterans here and establish a remarkable victory. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." So, will you become veterans? "Yes." Will you or won't you? "We will."

Until now, the only place where women have been trained to fight is in the communist world. Then in the Jewish nation and Korea. In Korea, women went out to fight. Have women fought on the battlefield anywhere else? Historically, that has not happened, but you can go out and fight? "Yes." With what? Do you want to fight with your butt? Do you want to fight with your chest? (Laughter) With what do you want to fight? You must fight with the fact that you have enemies of love. The enemies of love. They are enemies of my love, more than God's love. When you get married and live happily, if someone comes and cuts your husband's neck, will you just say, "Well, that's life," and stay quiet? "No." When you see the man who killed your husband, if he looks good and is handsome, and you think he is ten times better than your husband, will you turn around and say that was a good thing? "No." What do you mean no? If American women see a man who is a little better looking...

Did you love? You only wanted to receive love; you should have given love. Have you ever loved with your life on the line? American women are all like that. So to train American women, you have to do it the Eastern way. In the Eastern way, if a wife doesn't listen, you hit her. You should meet such a man and get educated, let's see. Then you would probably divorce right away! (Laughter)

What are you doing with a love that is not even as strong as a fist? Even if you hit, you should say, "Oh, please don't do that," (gesturing, laughter) and not let go; otherwise, what can you do with a love that is weaker than a single hit? "Even if you cut my neck, I won't let go." That's how it should be. I want to create such women. Do you understand what I mean?

What kind of woman do you want to be? Do you want to be a cheap woman who gets divorced with just one hit? Do you want to be a woman who, no matter what, wants to love with her life on the line? What do you want? "The second one." 

Now, raise your hands if you want to be that kind of woman. Hmm! If that's true, all the handsome men in America will want to take Unification Church women. Then, will you go for a good-looking husband from outside, or an ugly Unification Church husband? (Laughter) What will you do? "Unification Church husband." Why? Because he can be a companion in repaying my enemies. That is how the teacher chooses a spouse. Even though there were many famous, wonderful, and rich daughters when choosing a mother, I chose the current mother.

The sound of God's love must resonate throughout the universe. We must become a universe that lives intoxicated by the sound of God's love. However, the world has not yet heard the sound of love.

Think about it. If God looked at the five oceans and six continents of the earth, would He think they are beneath His feet, or would He think, "Oh, how big"? That's why if God steps one foot in Asia and one foot in Europe and dances, think about what will happen to this land. (Applause) Think about it. How would it be?

However, in this universe, we have not yet seen God dancing centered around love, we have not heard the sound of singing, and we have not seen love overflowing from God. Isn't that true? I want that kind of God; I don't want a God who sits on a throne in a traditional church and says, "Hey, you!" 

When you ask women, "Do you want to be the wife of a famous judge?" no one raises their hand. Why? Why? Why? Love comes after judgment; judgment cannot exist without love.

But God should love the world first and then judge, but because of the fall, He ended up judging first and loving later. It is perfectly fine to judge first to love. Therefore, the God of traditional churches is a judging God, and the God of the Unification Church is a loving God. So even if I grab God's beard and say, "Hoo hoo hoo," He doesn't say, "Hey, you!" but rather "Hee hee hee." (Laughter) Don't you want to see that?

We must liberate God. Among the Unification Church members, the statement that you must find your divorced parents again with your own hands also holds true. It's the same. You have a mission to liberate God and your parents.

Let's not miss the time.

So, what kind of connection do we have? We have a connection to repay the enemies of love. Do you understand? If you don't do it, you must know that your children and descendants in the future will have to pay a much greater price, no matter how much training you undergo that is like actual combat. War training, you know. No matter how good the results of war training are, it is of no use. It is not even as good as a small neighborhood war. You cannot feel the value of victory, the joy of victory, and the sorrow of defeat. "Are you talking about training?" (Interpreter) That's right. No matter how big the training is, even if the US Eighth Army is conducting training in Korea, it is of no use. You cannot feel the reality of winning or losing in a fight to take a neighborhood from enemies. You cannot feel the unfairness and joy of winning and losing in a small war. 

Do you understand? "Yes." Can it be compared to that?

What we are doing now is the last war, the last war. Therefore, if we miss this time, no matter how many hundreds or thousands of times we try to wage war again, it will not be possible. After this time passes, even if ten or a hundred countries focus on doing this in New York, it will be of no use. Therefore, the table where you eat, the place you sit, the street you walk on is the battlefield of heaven. It is the most serious battlefield in history. So even if bullets rain down, we must repay heaven's enemies. Do you understand? "Yes."

What I said yesterday is that the home church will be the base in the future. We are going to blow it up based on that. It's either someone igniting it or pushing the button; it's one of the two. Spring
Everyone, it is now spring. I don't think anyone dislikes spring. Is that right? "Yes." That's what I think.

Spring has the power of rebirth and the power of action. Young people who do nothing, or those in their teenage years attending school, will have an even greater stimulus towards spring. Those who appreciate spring and feel affection for it are those people.

On the other hand, older people, those who have responsibilities at home or in society, those who go out to work, when spring comes, even though it is the same spring, it will be a bit different because they have to work with responsibilities.

Then, older people who have educated their children and sent them off to marriage, becoming grandparents, when they greet spring, it will also be different. They will be filled with nostalgia. Therefore, when spring comes, such people will long for the past, reflecting on their youth and middle age, and it will be a good stimulus for them to reflect again. I think spring can be such a season. Even if the environment is different, it is the same that people will enjoy, appreciate, reflect, or contemplate during spring.

Now, is it only people who feel this way? Animals feel the same. Think about it. In winter, snow accumulates. Especially in places like New York, where it snows a lot, animals like deer, foxes, bears, and even the smallest insects, when spring comes, they start new activities with new hopes. Spring is such a season. 

The same goes for birds. Until now, wherever they go, it has been unnatural to find food, and their existence has been constrained, but when spring comes, everything becomes natural. A new stage of life unfolds.

Because everything is newly vibrant in this atmosphere, if spring boasts, it boasts of having the power of rebirth and the power of vitality. From here, reborn, each in their own way, they start difficult tasks toward the future.

Now, you have seen the trees in Belvedere, right? The leaves have fallen, and everything looks chaotic and bare, but now the new buds are starting to emerge. No one dislikes new buds, right? "Yes." That applies to both young and old, and even to animals and birds. Especially migratory birds, depending on the climate, all move toward the spring hills where new buds are emerging.

Spring comes where there is love. 

There may not be migratory birds here, but which bird leaves the most impression on you among migratory birds? "Geese." There will be geese here. What else? Swallows, perhaps? Right? People in the city might not feel much about swallows, but in the countryside, they are very impressive. They build nests under eaves and near homes, which is very impressive.

Also, when birds like Canadian geese cry out, they make a honking sound. (laughter) The swallows, you see, are very interesting birds that give off an exotic vibe. When Americans see them, they might feel like they are similar to Eastern people. (laughter)

Look at them. With their black backs and white decorative feathers, they look like wedding attire. They resemble a groom at a wedding, very much like a man in a black morning coat with a white shirt and a nice tie. Also, when you see two of them sitting and chirping, it is very romantic. Birds, you see, do not sing alone. When they sing, they either sing together or call to each other. That's how the songs unfold.

People are probably the same. Isn't that right? When you listen to songs, there are love songs, songs depicting happiness, and songs depicting peace. Therefore, where there are songs, there is love, and where there is love, spring comes. This is what comes to mind. Do you think so? "Yes."

Moreover, in the Unification Church, are there more older people or younger people? "Young." When you say "young," it feels like a fresh start, but when you say "old," it feels different. (making a face. Laughter) You all feel that way, right? The sound of "wong wong wong" resonates with youth. Then the sound of "buh-woong" sounds like an old, clunky car. (laughter)

The characteristic of the Unification Church is that young people gather. When you see the young people of the Unification Church, this young generation is like spring. Isn't that right? When you look at their faces, they all shine with the light of spring, filled with hope as everything is reborn and new buds emerge. Do you agree? "Yes." 

When you sit, do you have to slouch like this or sit up straight? (demonstrating) New buds are coming out...

Yesterday and Today
For people living in this world, there is a history of the past, and through today, there is a future. Just as it is for individuals, it is the same for families, nations, and the world, and it is also the same for heavenly providence. Therefore, between yesterday and today, there must be remnants of the past and present. History remains.

A desolate human world centered on selfish desires
Now, when you look at the Unification Church, you will realize that there is a difference between the time before entering the Unification Church and today after entering. So, let us think again about the two worlds, the two positions of the past and today after entering the Unification Church.

Is the Unification Church better, or was the past better? Before entering the Unification Church, you lived centered on yourselves. You lived centered on yourself, your siblings, your parents, your relatives, then if you were in America, as an American, and then as a person in the world. Everything you ate, slept, felt, and thought was confined to the perspective centered on yourself. If you had success or hope, it was the hope of becoming someone in that country.

When looking at people, there are three great desires. One is the issue of money, one is the issue of knowledge, and one is the issue of power. In these three areas, people pursue something. You will belong to one of these three areas and live within the boundaries of yourself. The world is further away than America. And America is further away than your own tribe. And your tribe is further away than your family, and your family is further away than yourself.

Although these concepts seem interconnected, the real question is how much responsibility you have in relation to them. Therefore, when you look at the whole, there is the world, there are nations, there are societies, there are religions, and there are families, but in the midst of all that, there is the existence of "me." You are at the center.

While doing this, whether there is heaven or not, whether God exists or not, and what the foundation of your own being is, you do not think about it and live like an animal, just dying as you are. That is life. Even if you get married, you marry for your own benefit. Even if you have children, you have them all for yourself. You think of your children centered on yourself. When you think about how fathers think this way, mothers think this way, and sons and daughters think this way, you can feel how desolate it is. It is a world as desolate as grains of sand.

Money does not guarantee human dignity and life
Now, let’s say we earned money and became millionaires. If you work hard, passing through your twenties into your thirties, forties, fifties, and sixties, you cannot become a millionaire without about thirty years of effort. Let’s say you became a millionaire at sixty. But when you reach sixty, the day of departure is not far off. Because you liked money, you earned it until you turned sixty, and now you must retire. 

When you look at the pile of money as a millionaire, will it be hopeful or despairing? What do you think? When you think about the past, isn’t it a shocking reality? When you think about the money you earned, it is astonishing. Concluding that you have lived your whole life for money is extremely miserable, isn’t it?

Moreover, if you have money, managing that money becomes a problem. When you reach the age of seventy without any heirs, there will be all sorts of internal troubles in companies, with schemes and slanders. When you look at such facts, how shocking is that? So, when you reach seventy or eighty and the day of death comes, all the money you earned becomes shattered. Standing in that position, reflecting on your life leads to a shocking conclusion. Will it be inherited as you wished, and will it remain as something valuable that you put your heart into when you earned it? Generally, it cannot remain that way.

People say that the teacher is one of those who have money, but you must feel well that money does not guarantee your dignity and your life.

If you have put several hundred thousand dollars into a safe, you won’t be able to sleep. You cannot sleep. To protect it, it would be better not to have it. When you know that several hundred thousand dollars is in there, you think a thief will come in, so you cannot sleep at night and must guard it. While guarding it, you do not know when you will die. You reach the conclusion that you must protect it at the risk of your life. You must know that you have to risk your life to protect it.

Among our families in Korea, one of the 36 families was entrusted with about five million won, which is about ten thousand dollars, and they said they couldn’t sleep at night because of having to guard it. (laughter) If ten thousand dollars causes that, imagine how it would be with a hundred thousand or a million dollars. They feel like they might go crazy. (laughter) You all are the same. Think about it. That is how it is. Money is not good. What good does it do? What good is there in that?

Knowledge does not bring happiness and comfort
Next, you are studying... You are going to some university and becoming a doctor, making a fuss about it. You tie yourself up with homework, eat poorly, do not play, do not rest, and stay up all night studying to earn a doctorate. And then you become a Nobel Prize winner and are called a great person in the world, but when you look at yourself quietly, there are many miserable things. It is the same, the same. No matter how much you become a Nobel Prize winner, having knowledge is just a narrow specialty. In this vast world, you have drilled a small hole to know about that field and are confined within that fence. When you look at the world and see the whole, you are extremely small. You may boast about what you know, but you know only a minuscule amount.

When you think about that, does knowledge bring happiness and comfort to humans? No, it does not. Knowledge means that the more you study, the more you realize how much you do not know. You come to know that there is even more that you do not know.

Now, go ahead and try to become a famous professor after entering school. Imagine spending your whole life just holding chalk, writing, and taking notes... Think about it. Even if you shout loudly while eating chalk dust, it only matters in that field; it does not affect the world, and you do not know how the world is changing. You have no room to think about how to change the world. You have no room to think about a single purpose. You know less than those who do not know. You are deeper into it...

When you think about that, even if you have knowledge, you spend your whole life just being a bookworm... You do not have confidence in yourself; you just gather what others say in that field and compare and study... That is a miserable state. Therefore, what you claim becomes vague. You have no confidence. Moreover, if you become a famous scholar, what does that mean? It is too precious to invest your life and your whole being into it.

Power cannot solve human problems
Then what is next? Next is power. Everyone dreams of being the president of this country at least once, right? What do they dream of? Power, strength. Let’s say you have held that power. Does it last forever? The president of the United States serves for four years; think about that. It is like blinking in the historical process. It is nothing more than that. You eat, dance, and do whatever, but it feels like a crazy mood. Even if it feels good, once it ends, it is nothing. Who comes to recognize it? It is worse than being a commoner. Go somewhere and drink freely, dance, and roam as you please. Oh, being a president... Everyone is like that. Such a person lives in a corner. Everyone pays attention to them, and being in the spotlight is burdensome.

Who is the wife of President Kennedy? Jackie! Think about it. Are there any American women who like Jackie? "No." Why not? Because she can marry freely and do well. (laughter) Looking at it this way, what is it? There is no power that lasts even ten years. Even when you hold that power, were you truly happy? No, not at all. It is a headache. The Path of the Chosen 
Today, I will speak on the topic of the Path of the Chosen. 
Tradition is established in the place where life and death are exchanged. 
Even when looking at your family, there are siblings and parents with various personalities. Then, when considering what kind of tradition is inherited from ancestors in that family, it is natural that a person with a character suitable for that ancestral tradition will inherit it. Also, when looking at a family, the person who can inherit all the possessions of the parents is someone who matches the character of those parents. 
When a tradition is established, if it is in England, for example, when it is said that the tradition of England has been established, all citizens must love their country and love one another according to that tradition. From this perspective, the place where tradition is established is a place where life and death are exchanged. It is established in a place of suffering, a difficult place, and we can roughly infer that this becomes the tradition of that nation. 
Tradition is established in a place where a nation either collapses or thrives, meaning it is established in a place where there is a high possibility of collapse but does not collapse. Of course, while tradition is established in difficult places, we must understand that those difficult places are not for the sake of the individual but for the sake of the whole. 
The same applies to inheriting a parent's property. If a parent has worked hard and suffered to possess that property, the child who can understand the parent's suffering and overcome even greater hardships will be the one to inherit from the parent. And it is only natural that the person who utilizes and consumes that property is not someone who uses it for themselves but someone who can utilize it for the entire family. 
To inherit God's tradition, one must break existing traditions. 
There are many countries in the world. Among those countries, which country possesses the tradition that humanity should carry? This is a tradition that anyone, any country should possess. If God exists, then God thinks about how to develop culture through some country on this earth by inheriting the heavenly tradition, so every country must hope for a nation that possesses the tradition that God desires from its own position. 
From this perspective, God has placed religions before humanity to bring fallen humans, who have become distanced from God, closer to God and to establish them in a position similar to God's, so that the individual, family, tribe, and nation can eventually unite the world completely. **History and Our Responsibility**

Are all the seminary students here? "A couple of them didn’t come, but everyone else is here." No, not all the seminary students are here. "Not everyone came." Those who attended the meeting yesterday are all here, right? 

From now on, you must have learned through yesterday's meeting that we are starting the second 40-day period anew. 

I will talk a bit under the title "History and Our Responsibility." 

Due to the fall, humanity is under the dominion of Satan. 

We have learned that because of the fall, God's creation must be restored. In other words, it means going through a process and then returning to the original position. That is restoration. Just as creation was, the history of humanity today, all of human history, is flawed, and therefore it must be indemnified and restored. It is the same. 

In other words, we cannot just leave everything that humanity has gone through over the past 4 billion people and a long history; we must either negate it or overcome it and transcend it to turn back. This includes individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the whole. 

When we focus on individuals, every single person must return. Thousands, tens of thousands must all return. Everyone must return. Therefore, we must go through all the principles of creation. 

The owner of this created world should be God, but due to the fall, it has become Satan. Also, all of human history has entered under Satan's dominion. You must always know this. Therefore, we must clearly understand the concept of Satan, that we are under Satan's control, and that we are within Satan's dominion. Those who do not clearly understand this cannot have a proper religious life. 

For example, during World War II, if a British soldier was captured by the German army and was in a prisoner of war camp, even though it is the same Europe, the living conditions are different. The lifestyle is different, and at the same time, the countries are different, and the environments are all different. The history is different, and everything is different. A British person knows that they have lived in Britain, so they know that it is currently a camp and always wants to escape. They yearn for freedom and strive to get out. Our Reunion  
Today, I will speak under the title "Our Reunion."  
A person does not come into this world by their own plan. Among those born as women, there are some who think, "Why was I born a woman? I wish I had been born a man." What about men? There might be men who think, "Ah, I wish I had been born a woman..." What do you think? Do you think there are many who wish they had been born as a man, or many who wish they had been born as a woman? (Laughter)

In countries like America, some even say that women are queens and men are subjects. American women might be strong like Doris. Small but strong. (Laughter)

Moreover, women think, "I was born a woman, but I look like a man, so this is wrong. If I were to be born a woman, how wonderful it would have been to be born beautiful!" They think like that, right? And those who were born as men think, "Ah, I was born a man, but I look like a woman, what can I do? I wish I had been a strong, bull-like man." Even men who look gentle think like that. Isn't that so?  
There is always a reason for people to meet.  
And men have beards while women do not. When you look at it this way, it seems that they are not meant to meet with those who are the same. They are meant to meet with those who are relatively opposite. When we go out into the world, we can see couples where the man is very handsome, but the woman is hunched over and looks disheveled. When women walk like that, it really looks bad. (Demonstrating with actions. Laughter) They walk like this... Yet they still meet and live together. Looking at the world, it is indeed strange.  
If you look at British people, some have bright blue eyes, black eyebrows, and bright yellow hair. Such people exist. (Laughing) It can happen. Some people have black hair as babies, but as they grow, their hair becomes yellow. That’s how it is.  
Then why aren’t eyebrows as long as hair? Wouldn't it be nice if eyebrows were this long? Why is that? Eyebrows keep falling out. They keep falling out before they get long, but as they age, they stop falling out, so they become longer. (Laughter) That’s why eyebrows...

Eyebrows must be black.

It is a principle that it should be fulfilled in my generation, but if there is someone who says they will continue even beyond their generation, God will favor that person. Do you understand what I mean?

That is why it is the same when you are working. We do not work for our own generation alone; we work to lay the foundation for the peace and happiness of our descendants for thousands and tens of thousands of generations in the future. Therefore, the more complicated it is, the more effort we must make to digest it all, and we must recognize that God's providence is being carried out through those who endure and wait. Do you understand?

When a woman lives with her husband and sees that he is incompetent, she feels burdened. However, instead of abandoning him, she thinks, "Since my husband is incompetent, I must support him," and continues to live with him. Reflection  
This morning, let's talk about the topic of 'reflection.'  
Every individual is born bearing the responsibility of their era. Just as it is for a person, the same goes for a nation. Every nation inevitably appears with a mission. Furthermore, this world, this single planet, also exists as a world that is necessarily related to some responsibility.  
All beings exist with some responsibility.  
Then, the question arises of what standard everyone—nations, individuals, and the world—moves according to. Can the purpose desired by an individual, the mission desired by a nation, and the mission desired by the world be the same or different? We cannot help but think about such questions.  
When an individual is born with some responsibility and carries out their mission, no matter how right that mission may seem in that era, it will inevitably be evaluated when it conflicts with the national perspective. If the individual goes this way and the nation goes that way, it will inevitably be criticized and removed in front of the direction the nation is heading.  
According to the same principle, if a nation is going this way but conflicts with the direction the world is heading, it will inevitably be evaluated here and will either retreat or cease to exist.  
If the world is moving in a direction that does not align with the direction of the entire universe, and if there is a transcendent God who governs providence, even if the world is guided by an excellent nation centered around the current people, if that direction does not align with God's direction, it will inevitably be corrected or must retreat. That is how it is viewed.  
However, when it comes to God's will, there are various intentions within that will. There are intentions in the economic field, intentions in the church field, and various contents are established here. And even when viewed from the perspective of God's providence, the question arises of which direction that providence takes as its mainstream.  
God's mainstream thought is love.  
When we look at it this way, what would that mainstream be? Is it God's power? Is it the exercise of God's creative power? Is it miraculous signs? What is it? It is true that a value-oriented mainstream is needed that can be good for the whole world and the entire universe. Don't you think so?  
Then what would that be? Jesus said, "I am the way, the truth, and the life; no one comes to the Father except through me." The way means that even if there is a straight path from Scotland to London, once you go, that's it. Also, truth... Truth is good. What is truth? It is the ability to recognize equal value. Then it can recognize comparative value. Then, "I am the way, the truth, and the life..." but life is needed.  
Among these three, which is central? What would be central? Is life central? When it comes to truth, truth is relative. Now, as someone who possesses that life, I always think here that I said, "I am the way, the truth, and the life," but one thing is missing. Love is missing. I think this needs to be added in the era of the Unification Church. Establish love there... The way of love must remain forever. It is always necessary. If it is truth, what kind of truth is it? It is the truth of love. Then what kind of life is it? It is a life related to love. In this way, everything becomes one. Everything becomes one, but if love is excluded, nothing connects. Do you all think so?  
Then what would God's mainstream thought be? "Love." God's mainstream thought will be the thought of love. Now, if we decide that way, if Reverend Moon claims this, do you think God would agree, or would He say, "That's your thought, but my thought is different"? How would He think? "That is correct." What do you think? "He says it is correct." Do you have the ability to judge that? Do you have the ability? "Yes." Uh-huh. (Laughter) Even if you don't have that ability, if you confidently say "yes," it appears that you have the ability. (Laughter)  
Have you ever heard of a department of love while studying at school? (Laughter) Have you heard of it? What do you think? "I haven't heard of it." (Laughter) But how do you know? You haven't learned it. You haven't learned it. But when you talk about love, your mouth opens, your eyes widen, and everyone becomes lively. Is that right? "Yes." No matter how small a grandmother is, when she talks about love, she says, "Wow, that's good." With love at the center, a grandmother and a grandson can become one, and with love at the center, children can also become one. There is nothing that cannot become one. After love passes through, a unified value is formed. Do you think so? "Yes." Now, what about the relationship between God and people? How about the relationship between God and people compared to that of a grandmother and a grandson? "They become one." It's the same principle.  
Now, when we look at it this way, what can transcend all hierarchical relationships and horizontal relationships and embrace to make one? It is neither power nor truth. Nothing can do it, but it can be done with love. (Laughter) Do you acknowledge that? "Yes."  
Then how can the direction of the universe, the direction God is heading, the direction the world is heading, the direction the nation is heading, and the direction people are heading differ? This conclusion can be drawn. It can be concluded that the direction of the world for God's love, the way the world goes, is universal. Then will the way God goes and the way the world goes collide, or will they connect? "They will connect." Now, if God is coming from that side and our planet is coming from this side in the opposite direction, what will happen? Will they collide and flatten out? What do you think? What will happen? Without side effects, truth must all be compared, and the way must all yield, and it must be a question of who goes first, whether you or I, and the entire hierarchical and sequential relationship becomes an issue.  
However, when we look at the issue of love, everything is resolved. Even if they collide, they can still turn back. When different things collide without love, they retreat as a reaction, but love inherently has the power to attract each other. The gravitational force is strong. So they turn back. It is bound to turn back. Do you understand? "Yes." Therefore, this means that it will turn back while remaining.  
Now, just because God changes positions, does that mean, "Oh, I don't like it! I don't want to change positions with people!" Would that be the case? Would they say, "I like it"? Would they say it is better or worse? When people who love each other dance, do they dislike spinning around? Does this dance just spin around? Do they go up and down while dancing? How do they turn? (Expressing with gestures) What do you like? (Laughter) When you see dancing, isn't it so? When a man goes up, a woman has to look up, and when a man goes down, a woman has to look down... How three-dimensional is that interaction? The spectators also see it like this... (Laughter) Is that right? "Yes."  
God also wants to be under love rather than under law.  
From that perspective, love is indeed a problem. Therefore, if we only have the direction of love, even if we follow God, God will like it, and even if there is a direct collision with God, He will still like it. Furthermore, if the direction of the nation is... If the world goes to God with love, what kind of path is the nation taking? If the nation's path is the path of love, will it conflict with the path the world is taking and the path God is taking? It is the same.  
If the world is going this way, but the nation comes this way with love, what will happen? If a person who loves comes next to you and pulls your side, do you dislike it? Do you dislike it if they poke you in the side? Do you kick them away because you dislike it? "No." What about it? Even if the direction is opposite, if you go with love, you won't dislike it. When your butt touches, you sweep that butt. (Laughter) Is that right? Does it still connect? "Yes." (Laughter) It's the same.  
Then what about the path an individual takes? If someone says, "I will abandon everything I was doing and walk the path of love, a path that can embrace the universe and reach God," what will happen? Would God kick him away, chase him away, and lock him in a mountain valley? What will happen? Can God leave, can the world leave, can the nation kick him away? What do you think will happen? Will the nation or the world or God stop at that station? "They will stop." Will they really stop? "Yes."  
Then what direction should humanity, the world, and the universe establish based on? From this perspective, it concludes that love is undoubtedly the answer. That conclusion is a valid conclusion. Is that right? Does that seem right to you? "Yes."  
Now, then, who is more valuable, the person who says, "I will become a global scholar and live for England, knowing nothing of love and disliking it," or the person who says, "I am a scholar and know nothing, but I will go with love"? Which person do you think is more valuable? Who do you think is more valuable, the knowledgeable person or the loving person? The loving person? "Yes." Why? (Laughter)  
If there is love, it can carry England, it can carry the world, and it can carry God. That is the conclusion.
