In the past, it was done that way, but now it must change.

Until now, America has been arrogant, believing it dominates the whole world, treating the world carelessly, but that is not how it should be. Even if America treats the world carelessly, it must learn to respect the world more than itself. That is how America can survive. That is how America can be welcomed. Otherwise, both God and the people of the world will dislike it.
So, they take young people and throw them into the remote areas of Africa and say, “Become slaves! Be slaves of Africa!” Is that a good thing or a bad thing? “It’s a good thing.” What makes it a good thing? Because it is the path of love for the world, the path of the herald of love, that is why it can command them to go. If Reverend Moon were to take white people and make them serve black people as slaves and teach them to love, would God look upon that and praise it or condemn it? What would He say? “He would praise it.” That’s right. When we critically examine the past and present, we must correct history. Without correcting this with love, the world has no hope. This applies to individuals, nations, and the world alike. Do you understand?

The path to destruction
Now, let’s think about our Unification Church. You must know that there is a path for the Unification Church to fail in the future. The Unification Church can also fail. If the love for God departs, it will fail. Secondly, what is it? If you start thinking centered around yourself, it will fail. If you love centered around yourself, you will drift away from God’s love. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” I talk about this with my mother too. I sometimes tell her that if we think centered around ourselves and do not consider our family, we will fail. We must fail.

This time, when I called my mother to London…. (laughs) My mother has really suffered a lot. She suffered giving birth…. She also had a hard time during this last birth. She gave birth to eleven, but one went to the spirit world, so now there are ten. Having ten is the most precious thing, ten. That’s why I promised to give her a gift after she gave birth this time. I told her not to bring any clothes when she came here; I would buy everything for her. So I went to a clothing store and chose clothes for her. I bought ten pieces of clothing, one for each child. This is the first time I have done this. (Applause)

After that, I became worried. I thought that Doris, who follows my mother, should not have such thoughts. She might think, “If my mother is buying clothes here, let me go out and buy some clothes too!” That could happen. (laughs) “The teacher bought my mother ten pieces of clothing, why does he hate me for buying ten pieces?” That could happen. So I am saying this in a formal setting now. If you give birth to ten children, you should buy ten pieces of clothing for them. (laughs)

I buy clothes for my family every day…. That’s true. When I come to England from abroad with my family, I take all the leaders out and buy them clothes. Why do I buy clothes? Because I think that British clothes are the best in the world. What is good about them? I don’t think they are good at all. However, I know that when I take them out and buy them here in England, they are quite pleased. (laughs) Since I have the ability to do that, it is good to buy them. Isn’t it? Then they treat it as the greatest treasure for their whole life. There is no need to buy bad things. Buy good things.

My mother’s personality is to keep giving to others. When I asked her how she managed to buy good clothes for me in New York, she just smiled. She thinks she has many clothes, but she doesn’t. (laughs) So, wouldn’t you like it more if I gave you clothes that my mother wore rather than buying you clothes directly? Wouldn’t you like that? Do you understand what I mean? Whenever I go to France, I think I should buy about a thousand pieces of French clothing. How wonderful would it be to share that with a thousand people! (laughs) Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.”

In that sense, you don’t have to worry about me buying a lot of clothes for my mother in the future. The teacher himself feels the same way. This morning, I dressed like this, but I try not to dress up too much. I try to have some flaws in one place. That way, I feel comfortable. Otherwise, I don’t feel at ease. A person who cannot buy clothes for himself alone cannot eat at a fancy restaurant alone. I tend to eat and drink moderately when I go home. However, when guests come, whether from Japan or elsewhere, I take them to nice places to eat.

Isn’t that necessary for you in the future? You must do that when you become responsible people. You see, it would be nice if I buy for you, right? “Yes.” They will think, “That person is amazing! He only brings distinguished guests.” Because I take all the guests from various countries with me. Do you understand what I mean?

When ordinary people see it, they might say, “Oh, Reverend Moon is living well and eating well while making us suffer.” However, Reverend Moon has gone through more than you have suffered. He has graduated, you see, graduated. Do you understand what that means? Now, even if I say I don’t want to, it is time for you to take care of the teacher and take him to nice places. You have reached a time when you want that and can want that. Do you understand? “Yes.” You must start thinking like that.

Now, when thinking from the spirit world, do you think I was born on Earth to suffer, or how do you think I was born? What would God think? Do you think I was born to suffer? I went through hardship because Christianity opposed me, because Christianity opposed me. For 2,000 years, I have struggled to indemnify what Christianity sacrificed over 20 years.

That ended in 1976, so 1977, 78, 79, 80, 81, more than 4 years have been shortened. Until now, I have worked to save Christianity…. If by 1981 everything is indemnified and restored, there will be no way for Christianity to survive. Even now, before the end of the third seven-year course, we must meet in churches and denominations for Christianity to survive. Then it can survive. Otherwise, there is no way to survive. Everything will pass by.

So now I called Mr. Lee (Lee Jae-seok), who is working on the interdenominational movement, and gave him special instructions. Do you understand what I mean? Aren’t they enemies? Enemies. But they are in the position of brothers. That is different. I do not eat, and I do not let you eat, but I feed those people. I am trying to save them. You are on the teacher’s side. You will not perish anyway. Do you understand what I mean?

If you have risen, you must know how to lower yourself, and if you have lowered yourself, you must know how to rise again to survive. 
Isn’t it in the Bible? There is the parable of the prodigal son, right? The second son wasted his inheritance in a far-off country and, having nothing to eat, ate what the pigs ate. When he returned to his parents, the parents welcomed him, but the elder brother was displeased that his parents welcomed his younger brother and complained, receiving rebuke from heaven and from his parents. It is exactly like that parable. When the ring was put on him, and he was dressed in fine clothes, and a feast was made with a calf, the elder brother complained. Similarly, “What is this ring? We have suffered so much, and what is this? You should treat us better.” That could be the Unification Church. Do you understand? “Yes.” Amen? “Amen.”

Even if we suffer, we must be prepared to pay the price. Even if you suffer, you should spend all your money to save them. That is good. Do you understand? That is the Unification Church. Because we are going the path of restoration centered on love based on principled standards toward all the Christians who opposed us in the past, the Unification Church will not perish; the whole world will accept the Unification Church. If Reverend Moon and his wife, as parents, are looked up to by everyone, and if that is the only good thing, the world will perish. You must also know how to live humbly at the bottom.

If it is a mother, she should not just like to keep receiving gifts; she should be able to say she is fine without receiving gifts. If that is not possible, if there is no prospect for that, then she will not receive gifts. The teacher will not give gifts. If there is no prospect for that, the mother will not receive anything either. That is the kind of person the teacher is. Do you like that? Women, answer me. Is that a good thing or a bad thing? Only the women should answer. “It is a good thing.” If the mother were to go around asking for gifts wherever she goes, what should we do? Should we give her gifts or not? “We should not give her gifts.” You know that well.

The teacher thinks that way too. As I become more famous, what will happen? After that, I think I should walk around with a bundle, traveling across the rivers and mountains. I think it would be wonderful to walk around the five oceans and six continents. How wonderful would that be? Would there be people following me or not? “There would be.”

If you do not know how to lower yourself after rising, and if you cannot engage in the movement of lowering yourself after rising, you will perish. You have no choice but to perish. Also, if a person in a low position does not try to rise, that person will also perish. That person has already perished. So when I look at Africans or anyone else, I see it from that perspective. I wonder if these people want to play and live. I think we must make them work harder to rise, even if it means making them suffer. They must know how to turn back.

The Earth also turns, and because night and day change, it is welcomed for thousands of years. It is welcomed by all things. Do you understand? “Yes.” The Earth is like that, history is like that, the world is like that, and God must also be welcomed in the same way.

Now, if we look at our Unification Church from the past to the present, our Korean headquarters has risen significantly compared to the past. However, the Koreans are trying to rise without acknowledging the foundation that the teacher has laid. Koreans are trying to rise just like that, but that cannot happen. You must not have that mindset. Therefore, when coming to Western society, you must be prepared to suffer for the Western people. If not, do not come! It must be done that way. If Korea incurs a lot of debt in the future, if Korea receives help, it must help a lot. We must engage in that kind of activity. It must return to that, do you understand what I mean? “Yes.”

You must evaluate your entire life based on public standards, determining what position you stand in now and what position you will stand in the future, and you must be able to decide how you should act in accordance with that principle.

Moreover, this period of the third seven-year course is a period of suffering, a period of suffering. Once this period passes, there will be no more suffering to endure. Our Unification Church members must let the world know that they have suffered for it. High or low, everyone must know that. Do you understand? Has that been known until now, or not? “It has not been known.” Until it is fully ripe, the Unification Church must do that, until it is ripe. There, the five races have worked together.

In this context, what is indispensable in the Unification Church? What kind of love are we talking about? It is about loving the world with God’s love. Are you trying to move with God’s love? Are you moving? “We are moving.” Are you trying to do it? How is it? “We are doing it.” That is your thought. I am asking whether I am doing this or not. Have you done it with God’s love? Are you doing it or will you do it? It must be that you have done it and are doing it until now. 

Gifts to bring to God
Now reflect on this. When you are hungry, do you say, “Oh, I am hungry!” But have you thought about whether England is spiritually hungry? How is it? Is England spiritually full? When you go before God in the spirit world, what gift can you bring? There is nothing. Not money, not the honor of a PhD on this earth, not the love of your beloved husband, not living well, none of that. Those things cannot be gifts. What is it? You must bring love for the world and for God. That is what remains. What does John 3:16 say? “For God so loved the world…” Does it say God loves the world or that He loves individuals? “The world.” Did it say the Unification Church or the world? “The world.” It says He loves the world. That is why He gave His only begotten Son. The only begotten Son came to love the world.

Therefore, because we believe centered on love, we do not perish. We are saved. The owner loves the world, so we must love the world together. What about Christianity now? Christianity has all fallen apart under the name of denominations. Isn’t that right? There is no thought of how the world is or how God is. They are perishing while only loving their own denomination and their own country. When we look at this Christianity that is perishing, we must love the world and God beyond denominations and nations.

Next, if communism sweeps the world and can lead humanity to extinction, the Unification Church, being a religion, must say to love the enemy to prevent that.
Should we fight with guns? What will you do? Will you fight and block them, or will you have the ability to surpass them in every aspect so that they cannot resist? Among those two options, what will you choose? Will you fight to block them, or will you increase all your strength to stop them? Which one should we pursue? "Increase strength..." Is that easy? "No." The Communist Party started in 1917 and built itself over 60 years. Are you willing to wait more than 60 years? "No." Then will you do it in 6 years? 3 times 6 equals 18; will you do it in 18 years? How many years will it take? If you want to achieve it in one-third of the time, you must suffer more than three times as much. You need to put in more than three times the effort. That is the realistic problem.

Now, should the members of the Unification Church rest or not? "They should not rest." After the Bolshevik Revolution, young people working in the Soviet Communist Party went without food and lived on gruel to get through the third five-year plan. They suffered so much that they couldn't even hold a pen. The global movement was centered around those who survived that. Do you understand what I mean? A week of fasting is nothing for you.

If you truly become a Bolshevik party member, you must kill the bourgeois parents. They even created a group for killing parents. To prove that you are a Communist as a bourgeois son, you must kill your bourgeois father. Do you understand that? Lenin said, "If you lie more than a hundred times, it becomes the truth." Have you acted with a clear conscience until now? It is purely Satanic.

All communist propaganda methods are like that. That is why the democratic world is being deceived by it. Do you think the Communist Party keeps international agreements? Those who think so are foolish. They are willing to destroy the democratic world and the bourgeois class by any means necessary. They believe that all victories lie at the end of the barrel of a gun. Do you understand? God is not like that. All victories are seen as being in love. It is different. Do you understand? That is why the communist world is increasingly filled with fear. Global fear is looming.

So what about the Unification Church? Do you work because you are afraid of Reverend Moon, or do you work because you long for God's love? "I long for God's love." When you suffer centered on love, the value increases exponentially. It has a three-dimensional quality, a three-dimensional quality.

You are recognized for having loved God, and you should love your parents, siblings, and nation. In that sense, if you want to do better than the Communist Party within 20 years, you must work three times harder than they do. "Communists, you grow at night! We work even at night!" You must think this way. You have to. When looking at England, you should say, "If you want to sleep, sleep; if you want to play, play," while we do not do that. Did you come here to sightsee? "No." Then why did you come? You came to be a guide for those people. You came to find the way of love. What an amazing guide that is. Is that something to be ashamed of? "No." Shouldn't you be proud of it? It is different. Do you understand? "Yes."

Have I done this centered on love? Am I doing it? Will I do it? Let's leave that aside. It is now certain. It has been said that it is good to give everything for God. Then, loving God means being a filial child to your parents, being a loyal subject to your nation, and being a saint to the world. Which is more valuable: loving God directly or loving Him through being filial to your parents, loyal to your nation, and a saint to the world? What do you think? You must answer that clearly. What do you think? "Being filial to parents..." Is that really true? "Yes."

But there is a condition. Then you must set conditions. What is the difference between saying, "I will love our parents on this earth in place of God" and just saying, "I will love my parents and love God"? Which does God want more? "In place of God..." Why? Why? Because God is a principled God. If a son loves Adam and Eve, he must have the perspective that he loves his parents because God wants it this way. That is principled.

Also, when it comes to loving the nation, you must love as a son of God. That is the principle. You must love as a son of God loves God. Therefore, you must do even more. Furthermore, when it comes to loving the world, you must also love as a son of God. That is the principle.

However, what happens after the Fall? It means that you did not connect with God's love. Therefore, you must give up everything and cling only to God. That is for the purpose of restoration through indemnity. Do you understand? You must understand that the need for indemnity arose because of the Fall. You must realize that it is necessary because of the Fall. If there had been no Fall, serving your parents in place of God would be connecting with Him. If there had been no Fall, serving the king of the nation would lead to heaven. Do you understand?

Have you ever said that you love only God? Have you? "Yes." Until you receive God's recognition, you cannot love your parents or your nation. You must follow the path that allows you to love the world and love only God.

That is why our fallen descendants could become parents and kings, but they could not become the masters of the world or the sons and daughters of God. Therefore, what does our Unification Church do? It does this. Let us give up everything, love the world, and love God! Let us love the world and return to God. After being recognized, when you become that, you return home to love. You love your parents as you love the world and as you love God. If you love the king of your nation like that, it becomes one nation. Do you understand what I mean?

You are to love your parents, siblings, and nation in place of God, with the qualification that God recognizes you for having loved the world and God. Then you will automatically become one. In that position, you can inherit everything. Adam and Eve could not love God and could not love God's ideal world. They could not do that and centered on themselves, they loved man and woman. They could not even serve their parents in the family. You must understand that development occurs through such a process centered on love.

Now, who are the ancestors of Adam and Eve? "God." Who are your ancestors? "True Parents." What are True Parents? Aren't they your mother and father? Your mother and father. How is our position? It is not different from Adam and Eve's position, is it? Adam and Eve were in a vertical relationship, and you are in a horizontal relationship. Therefore, you must first establish the vertical and then establish the horizontal relationship. To do that, you must cut this off. When you make a 90-degree angle, can you do it without standing this straight? Does the vertical come out? This is wrong... "It does not come out." Right? Do you understand what I mean?

In that sense, you are to become the sons and daughters of God, centered on the heavenly world. Then, since you are in a vertical relationship centered on God, you must establish that love and then establish horizontal love. The 90-degree relationship is recognized by God.

You should be grateful for sacrificing before God. 

If Adam and Eve had engaged in public love, there would have been no Fall, right? They fell while engaging in private love. You must align your nose. Do you understand? First, what must you do? "Vertical love." Then? "Horizontal love." You must think of vertical love, establish God's love vertically, and then prepare for the 90-degree love. The nation must also engage in this.

Have I ever been in such a time? "Yes." I am doing that work now. Have you not been able to love your parents? You are now returning to the global standard. You are returning to Korea. That is why I stopped by England. You are the same. You must walk this path.

You are not doing it over a long period; you are standing in such a position in a short time. The tree has grown this much, but what about you? The roots of my tree have come up this much, so I am grafting onto you. I am grafting. Do you understand what I mean? You must not go down from here; you must go up beyond this. You must love your nation, the world, and God. If you cut this off and stick it in, you must live. Can you live as a son of God? "Yes." Then it is possible.

That is why you must know that you are loving. If you cannot be someone who has loved and is loving, you will have no offering to bring to the heavenly kingdom. Therefore, you must set up 360 homes and experience loving the world and loving God. You must go to visit God in the position of love. You must understand that you are going to establish a tradition of love. You must go and teach love. Teach love. Do you understand what I mean?

You must clearly understand that you cannot stand in a position where you have loved, are loving, and can love. If you do not do that, no matter how much you may have to boast about in the past, it will not work. Everything will collapse. Do you understand, or not? "I understand."

What are you selling these days? Is there anyone fundraising here? Are you selling fish? (Laughter) Why are you selling fish? Aren't you catching fish to sell them all dead? (Laughter) If you sell for yourself, it is miserable. When a person more precious than fish dies, it is to save that person that you say, "You must sacrifice yourself, sacrifice in love." It is about dying for the sake of love for people. Then the fish cannot complain. Those who do not do that will perish more and more. They must be punished. Otherwise, God is the one who infringes upon the natural world. It must be fair.

When you eat meat, don't you feel sorry for the chicken? When you catch and eat the gentle lamb or the cow? For such a common purpose... Because of love, because you are doing it for God, because you are a loving person, you must connect to a higher love, and if that is the case, it is a joyful thing. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

So, after eating, should you sacrifice for God or not? "You must." After eating steak, should you run more or not? "You should run more." That is how it should be. That is the right way to think. Did you understand that clearly? "Yes."

So, when you catch fish to sell, explain it like this. When this fish goes into our mouths, say this. Think that you will think like this. When the fish goes into a person's mouth, what does it complain about? A person must also be grateful for sacrificing before the Lord God, and then the fish will also be grateful. (Laughter) Then how happy will that fish be? (Laughter) You must think about that even when you eat. Every time you take a spoonful, think like that, all of you. When you eat vegetables, can you just shove them in without greeting? What they oppose is also to make me sacrifice for God. 

Plant God's love in the world.

What is today's title? "Reflection." What should you evaluate based on? "Centered on love." You must evaluate with love for the world and love for God. Now, you all know that love. You all know it. Now, what is it? It is that you have done it and are doing it. It is not that you will do it. To think 'I will do it' is to think like an enemy. A fallen person must love the world and love God and return to love their parents and their nation. You must go around in a circle. Then wherever you go, you will be welcomed. In the past, you left and abandoned everything, so you were opposed, but now you will be welcomed wherever you go.

In the future, when this three-stage seven-year course ends, all the young people who have entered the Unification Church, Americans, those who left home and became hippies, will all be sent back. Where will they be sent? They will all be sent back home. Then how much will they praise the Unification Church? They will go and be filial to their parents, love their relatives, and love their nation. Now they are all abandoning everything because they are being scorned and robbed.

In the future, there will come a time when religious believers will no longer be persecuted. We are now in a time when we are overcoming such a process. By loving the world and God, you will be able to win in everything because of the position of having loved and being in love in the future.

No matter where you work or what you do, you must think that you are sacrificing yourself to love the world and God.

Such a person will find even the first person they meet to be good for no reason. Such a person, when they see that face, will think, "Ah, I hope that person comes back!" It will definitely be like that. "I hope they come back! Where have they gone? I hope to meet them again!" They will think like that. Then, "Well, that person said they were from the Unification Church, so if I go to the Unification Church, I might meet them!" They will come looking. But when they come, they will find many people like that. Then they will think, "If I become a member of the Unification Church, I will become like that." Do you understand? That is precious. It is precious. God's love...

Even when you are fundraising, you must think that you are doing it to share love for the world and God's love, to educate. So do not set a price for the fish; say, "Give what you want." Then, if you plant that love, you can give hundreds or thousands of times. You must go around planting love, and if you want to repay the value of that love, do so with the heart to repay. If you go to twenty houses a day instead of ten, you are planting even more love. If you go to a hundred houses or two hundred houses, you are planting as much love as you go. Then you will not be tired even if you run around all day. You will not be tired even if you run around all day.

Then, when that person rings the bell in that neighborhood, everyone will rush out into the street. Meeting people and greeting them is more enjoyable than buying fish. Those people are buying the fish of love. Do you understand what I mean? Even now, you can smell it from your hands, right? That is a boast. That is the smell of love for the purpose of loving. Do you understand?

Now, who will raise their hand to say, "I have loved, I am loving, and I will love"? You must discard the future. (Laughter) There is no need to say, "I will do it." That is unnecessary. Why do it? Because God does it, and the teacher does it, so we will do it too! It is the same. That is how it should be.
